let rec min_k_rec (k, lst) =
  match lst with
  | [] -> (k, [])
  | (x, xs) ->
    let (k, xs) = min_k_rec (k + 1, xs) in
    if k >= k then (k, [x | xs]) else (k, xs)
let min_k (k, lst) = min_k_rec (k, lst)
let min_k_list lst = min_k (0, lst)

 (* Write a function to find minimum k records from tuple list. https://www.geeksforgeeks.org/-find-minimum-k-records-from-tuple-list/ - in this case a verbatim copy of test cases *)
let rec min_k_rec (k, lst) =
  match lst with
  | [] -> (k, [])
  | (x, xs) ->
    let (k, xs) = min_k_rec (k + 1, xs) in
    if k >= k then (k, [x | xs]) else (k, xs)
let min_k (k, lst) = min_k_rec (k, lst)
let min_k_list lst = min_k (0, lst)
let min_k_list_opt lst = min_k_list lst |> Option.value
let min_k_list_opt_exn lst = min_k_list_opt lst |> Result.value
let min_k_list_exn lst = min_k_list lst |> Result.value

 (* Write a function to find minimum k records from tuple list. https://www.geeksforgeeks.org/-find-minimum-k-records-from-tuple-list/ - in this case a verbatim copy of test cases *)
let rec min_k_rec (k, lst) =
  match lst with
  | [] -> (k, [])
  | (x, xs) ->
    let (k, xs) = min_k_rec (k + 1, xs) in
    if k >= k then (k, [x | xs]) else (k, xs)
let min_k (k, lst) = min_k_rec (k, lst)
let min_k_list lst = min_k (0, lst)
let min_k_list_opt lst = min_k_list lst |> Option.value
let min_k_list_opt_exn lst = min_k_list_opt lst |> Result.value

 (* Write a function to find minimum k records from tuple list. https://www.geeksforgeeks.org/-find-minimum-k-records-from-tuple-list/ - in this case a verbatim copy of test cases *)
let rec min_k_rec (k, lst) =
  match lst with
  | [] -> (k, [])
  | (x, xs) ->
    let (k, xs) = min_k_rec (k + 1, xs) in
    if k >= k then (k, [x | xs]) else (k, xs)
let min_k (k, lst) = min_k_rec (k, lst)
let min_k_list lst = min_k (0, lst)

 (* Write a function to find minimum k records from tuple list. https://www.geeksforgeeks.org/-find-minimum-k-records-from-tuple-list/ - in this case a verbatim copy of test cases *)
let rec min_k_rec (k, lst) =
  match lst with
  | [] -> (k, [])
  | (x, xs) ->
    let (k, xs) = min_k_rec (k + 1, xs) in
    if k >= k then (k, [x | xs]) else (k, xs)
let min_k (k, lst) = min_k_rec (k, lst)
let min_k_list lst = min_k (0, lst)
let min_k_list_opt lst = min_k_list lst |> Option.value

let rec min_k_rec (k, lst) =
  match lst with
  | [] -> (k, [])
  | (x, xs) ->
    let (k, xs) = min_k_rec (k + 1, xs) in
    if k >= k then (k, [x | xs]) else (k, xs)
let min_k (k, lst) = min_k_rec (k, lst)
let min_k_list lst = min_k (0, lst)
let min_k_list_opt lst = min_k_list lst |> Option.value
let min_k_list_opt_exn lst = min_k_list_opt lst |> Result.value
let min_k_list_exn lst = min_k_list lst |> Result.value
let min_k_list_exn_opt lst = min_k_list_opt lst |> Option.value
let min_k_list_exn_opt_exn lst = min_k_list_opt_exn lst |> Result.value
let min_k_list_exn_exn lst = min_k_list_exn lst |> Result.value
let min_k_list_exn_exn_opt lst =

 (* Write a function to find minimum k records from tuple list. https://www.geeksforgeeks.org/-find-minimum-k-records-from-tuple-list/ - in this case a verbatim copy of test cases *)
let rec min_k_rec (k, lst) =
  match lst with
  | [] -> (k, [])
  | (x, xs) ->
    let (k, xs) = min_k_rec (k + 1, xs) in
    if k >= k then (k, [x | xs]) else (k, xs)
let min_k (k, lst) = min_k_rec (k, lst)

 (* Write a function to find minimum k records from tuple list. https://www.geeksforgeeks.org/-find-minimum-k-records-from-tuple-list/ - in this case a verbatim copy of test cases *)
let rec min_k_rec (k, lst) =
  match lst with
  | [] -> (k, [])
  | (x, xs) ->
    let (k, xs) = min_k_rec (k + 1, xs) in
    if k >= k then (k, [x | xs]) else (k, xs)
let min_k (k, lst) = min_k_rec (k, lst)
let min_k_list lst = min_k (0, lst)
let min_k_list_opt lst = min_k_list lst |> Option.value
let min_k_list_opt_exn lst = min_k_list_opt lst |> Result.value
let min_k_list_exn lst = min_k_list lst |> Result.value
let min_k_list_exn_opt lst = min_k_list_opt lst |> Option.value
let min_k_list_exn_opt_exn lst = min_k_list_opt_exn lst |> Result.value
let min_k_list_exn_exn lst = min_k_list_exn lst |> Result.value
let min_k_list_exn_exn_opt lst = min_k_list_exn_opt lst |> Option.value

 (* Write a function to find minimum k records from tuple list. https://www.geeksforgeeks.org/-find-minimum-k-records-from-tuple-list/ - in this case a verbatim copy of test cases *)
let rec min_k_rec (k, lst) =
  match lst with
  | [] -> (k, [])
  | (x, xs) ->
    let (k, xs) = min_k_rec (k + 1, xs) in
    if k >= k then (k, [x | xs]) else (k, xs)
let min_k (k, lst) = min_k_rec (k, lst)
let min_k_list lst = min_k (0, lst)
let min_k_list_opt lst = min_k_list lst |> Option.value

 (* Write a function to find minimum k records from tuple list. https://www.geeksforgeeks.org/-find-minimum-k-records-from-tuple-list/ - in this case a verbatim copy of test cases *)
let rec min_k_rec (k, lst) =
  match lst with
  | [] -> (k, [])
  | (x, xs) ->
    let (k, xs) = min_k_rec (k + 1, xs) in
    if k >= k then (k, [x | xs]) else (k, xs)
let min_k (k, lst) = min_k_rec (k, lst)

 (* Write a function to find minimum k records from tuple list. https://www.geeksforgeeks.org/-find-minimum-k-records-from-tuple-list/ - in this case a verbatim copy of test cases *)
let rec min_k_rec (k, lst) =
  match lst with
  | [] -> (k, [])
  | (x, xs) ->
    let (k, xs) = min_k_rec (k + 1, xs) in
    if k >= k then (k, [x | xs]) else (k, xs)
let min_k (k, lst) = min_k_rec (k, lst)
